<p>Related to the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">jupe</i> and the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Old Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">jupa</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юбка.html>ю́бка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">júbka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юбка.html>ю́бки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юбка.html>ю́бки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юбка.html>ю́бок</a></b>)

***ювелирный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ювелирный.html>ювели́рный</a> (14876)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ювелир.html>ювели́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">juvelír</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ювелирный.html>ювели́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">juvelírnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jewelry</li>
<li>jeweler's</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fine, minute, well-made, intricate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ювелирный.html>ювели́рно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">juvelírno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***юг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>юг</a> (2073)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">югъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jugŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jugъ</i>. Displaced <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">угъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>юг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jug</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>ю́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>юга́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>юго́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>south
<dl><dd><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уехать.html>уе́хать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>юга́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ujéxatʹ na <b>jugá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go to the south (e.g., to the Black Sea coast) for holiday</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>South — southern part of any region
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>ю́ге</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žitʹ na <b>júge</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to live in the South (of Russia)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> southerly wind
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:южный.html>ю́жный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">júžnyj véter</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>юг</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:веять.html>ве́ет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>гре́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jug</b> véjet, stárovo gréjet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A south wind blows, it warms an old man.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***южный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:южный.html>ю́жный</a> (1942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>юг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:южный.html>ю́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">júžnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)южне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)южне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">южне́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>south, southern</li>
<li>southerly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>юг</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***юлить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:юлить.html>юли́ть</a> (11103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юла.html>юла́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">julá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юлить.html>юли́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">julítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bustle, to fuss <i>(about)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play up <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wriggle</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:юнга.html>ю́нга</a> (20596)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Junge</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юнга.html>ю́нга</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">júnga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юнга.html>ю́нги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юнга.html>ю́нги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юнга.html>ю́нг</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cabin boy, ship's boy <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a boy serving on a ship</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1985</b>,  “Рыба-кит”, performed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yuliy_Kim" class="extiw" title="w:Yuliy Kim">Юлий Ким (Julij Kim)</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">ка́к-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:юнга.html>ю́нга</a></b> ду́дочкин / <a href = vnd.unilang:бросить.html>бро́сил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лот.html>ло́т</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удочка.html>у́дочку</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:клюнуть.html>клю́нул</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кашалот.html>кашало́т</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kák-to <b>júnga</b> Dúdočkin / Brósil v móre lót, / Í na étu údočku / Kljúnul kašalót.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Sometime, <b>Cabin Boy</b> Dudochkin / Threw into the sea a sounding line; / And at this line / bit the cachalot.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:юноша.html>ю́ноша</a> (2072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:юноша.html>ю́ноша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">junoša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">уноша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unoša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юноша.html>ю́ноша</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">júnoša</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юноша.html>ю́ноши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юноша.html>ю́ноши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юноша.html>ю́ношей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>youngster, male youth</li>
<li>young man</li></ol>

***юный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:юный.html>ю́ный</a> (1896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">юнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">junŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*junъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂yuh₁en-</i>. Displaced the inherited <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">унъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">оунъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юный.html>ю́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">júnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)юне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)юне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>young, youthful (in the early part of life or growth)</li>
<li>juvenile</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:юркий.html>ю́ркий</a> (13120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">юр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jur</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">busy place, market square; whirlpool, strong current</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>agile, nimble</li>
<li>quick, brisk <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a vehicle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***юркнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:юркнуть.html>юркнуть</a> (13283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юркий.html>ю́ркий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">júrkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юркий.html>ю́ркий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">júrkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юркнуть.html>юркну́ть</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юркнуть.html>ю́ркнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jurknútʹ</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">júrknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to whisk, to flit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:юркнуть.html>юркнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толпа.html>толпу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jurknutʹ</b> v tolpú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to plunge into the crowd</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:юродивый.html>юро́дивый</a> (23049)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">юродивъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jurodivŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p><span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology is incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юродивый.html>юро́дивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">juródivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eccentric, mad, whacky, nutty, mental; crazy, deranged, lunatic</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>поме́шанный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poméšannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудаковатый.html>чудакова́тый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čudakovátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">юродивость</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jurodivostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">юродствовать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jurodstvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юродивый.html>юро́дивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">juródivyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юродивый.html>юро́дивого</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юродивый.html>юро́дивые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юродивый.html>юро́дивых</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юродивый.html>юро́дивая</a></b>)

***ютиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ютиться.html>юти́ться</a> (17097)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A connection with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">jùmts</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roof</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">jùmt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to thatch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is one possibility. This etymology conflicts with the doctrine that *<i>JaN</i> became *<i>ję</i> in Proto-Slavic.
</p><p>ESSJa recontructs *<i>jutiti sę</i> instead, allegedly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*YewH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blend, mix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with a t-extension.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ютиться.html>юти́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jutítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to huddle, to huddle together, to take shelter</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приют.html>прию́т</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prijút</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уют.html>ую́т</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ujút</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:юшка.html>ю́шка</a> (31039)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юшка.html>ю́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">júška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юшка.html>ю́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юшка.html>ю́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юшка.html>ю́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>broth <i>(the liquid part of soup in which ingredients have been boiled)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люблю́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:юшка.html>ю́шку</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> бо́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́вится</a> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ща</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gúšča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne óčenʹ ljubljú <b>júšku</b>, mne bólʹše nrávitsja <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">gúšča</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gúšča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't like broth much, I like the solids more.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:юшка.html>ю́шка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:салат.html>сала́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>júška</b> saláta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">salad juice</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blood

***я.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> (6)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Letter_4">Letter</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ya_(Cyrillic)" class="extiw" title="w:Ya (Cyrillic)">Ya (Cyrillic)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ya_(Cyrillic)" class="extiw" title="w:Ya (Cyrillic)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ja</span>) (<i>lower case</i>, <i>upper case</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The thirty-third and final letter of the Russian Cyrillic alphabet. Its name is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and it has the sound of English <b>ya</b> in <i><b>ya</b>rd</i>. It is preceded by the letter <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">Ю</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Ju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The Cyrillic letter <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Ja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*(j)azъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*éǵh₂</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_3">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">I</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">first-person singular subject pronoun</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ja</b> rússkij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am Russian.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чное</a> местоимение <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:единственный.html>еди́нственного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числа</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:служить.html>слу́жит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обозначение.html>обозначе́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорящий.html>говоря́щим</a>, пищущим <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ябеда.html>я́беда</a> (21830)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">embætti</i>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌰𐌽𐌳𐌱𐌰𐌷𐍄𐌹</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">andbahti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">service, office</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ambahti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">position, office</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ябеда.html>я́беда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jábeda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ябеда.html>я́беды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ябеда.html>я́беды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ябеда.html>я́бед</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">masculine or feminine<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tattletale</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">feminine<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> slander, snitching</li></ol>
